{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define A\+V\+\_\+\+E\+F\+\_\+\+C\+R\+C\+C\+H\+E\+CK~(1$<$$<$0)}

Verify checksums embedded in the bitstream (could be of either encoded or decoded data, depending on the codec) and print an error message on mismatch. If A\+V\+\_\+\+E\+F\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+L\+O\+DE is also set, a mismatching checksum will result in the decoder returning an error.
